			category_id = "21";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword) == '%E7%A6%8F%E8%A2%8B'){
			category_id = "2101";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword) == '%E3%81%9D%E3%81%AE%E4%BB%96'){
			category_id = "2199";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword).match(/%E7%A6%8F%E8%A2%8B/)){
			category_id = "20";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword) == '%E3%83%9E%E3%82%BF%E3%83%8B%E3%83%86%E3%82%A3%E3%82%A6%E3%82%A7%E3%82%A2'){
			category_id = "2001";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword).match(/%E3%83%99%E3%83%93%E3%83%BC%E3%82%B0%E3%83%83%E3%82%BA/)){
			category_id = "2002";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword) == '%E3%83%93%E3%83%96'){
			category_id = "2003";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword) == '%E3%83%99%E3%83%93%E3%83%BC%E3%83%AD%E3%83%B3%E3%83%91%E3%83%BC%E3%82%B9'){
			category_id = "2004";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword) == '%E3%83%99%E3%83%93%E3%83%BC%E3%82%B7%E3%83%A5%E3%83%BC%E3%82%BA'){
			category_id = "2005";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword) == '%E3%83%99%E3%83%93%E3%83%BC%E7%94%A8%E5%93%81'){
			category_id = "2006";
		}
		else if(encodeURIComponent(keyword).match(/%E3%83%99%E3%83%93%E3%83%BC%E3%81%9D%E3%81%AE%E4%BB%96/)){
			category_id = "2099";
		}
		location.href = "https://web.mbkr.jp/category/" + category_id;
		return true;
	} else {
		return false;
	}



return true;
}
